###### NAVIGATE - BACK : [[B25]]

![[B25 ANNOUNCEMENT.svg]]



### **Kickstart your day at the [Tunerbash](https://tunerbash.ca/calgary/) Car Event at [Airdrie Air Park](https://www.google.ca/maps/place/Airdrie+Air+Park/@51.2660741,-113.9972922,13.25z/data=!4m6!3m5!1s0x5373e0131a06fa45:0x3cd5cb477793defd!8m2!3d51.27005!4d-113.9358596!16zL20vMDlxbm0x?entry=ttu).**
    
- [ ] Starts at 12 PM. [NOON]
- [ ] Enjoy car expos, races, and drift events.
- [ ] Check the images below for location and activity details.
- [ ] **[Ticket Required](https://www.showpass.com/tunerbashcalgaryopener/#location)**: A ticket is necessary for admission.
- [ ] **Transportation:** Arrange your own transportation to the car show.

<br><br/>
### **Curate your outfit for the evening.**
    
- [ ] Meet near Chinook at [Thriftopia](https://www.google.ca/maps/place/THRIFTOPIA/@51.0006961,-114.0717161,15.55z/data=!4m6!3m5!1s0x537170f9d7cfffff:0x1114894a9301b6e1!8m2!3d50.9967186!4d-114.0618061!16s%2Fg%2F11g9qf1x_w?entry=ttu) at 4 PM.
- [ ] Theme: "TIMELESS."
- [ ] Explore from three thrift stores options [closing time may apply].
- [ ] **Transportation:** Arrange your own transportation from the car show to the thrift stores or meet us directly at the thrift stores

<br><br/>
### **Evening Plans: Dinner and Bar Hopping.**
    
- [ ] Dinner at [Palomino Smokehouse](https://www.google.ca/maps/place/Palomino+Smokehouse/@51.0473532,-114.0726252,15.62z/data=!3m1!5s0x53716ffdd04e6f01:0xe1eb691994af4d2f!4m6!3m5!1s0x53716ffdce07956d:0x7123bb1890f2a02d!8m2!3d51.0463751!4d-114.063591!16s%2Fg%2F1wk6zfnm?entry=ttu) at 7 PM.
- [ ] Start bar hopping once feed.
- [ ] Bar locations will be decided during dinnerâ€”check the pictures for options.
- [ ] **Transportation:** We'll take the train together from the thrift stores to downtown.

<br><br/>
### **Join Us Anytime!**
    
- [ ] Bring some company and join us whenever it fits your schedule.
- [ ] Expect a day filled with fun, style, and unforgettable memories.

### Group Chat : [INSTAGRAM](https://ig.me/j/AbZ6sGfZ7nYz3hK1/)

<br><br/>
